e
 on Thursday

 Voting is going on today amid tight security, read some important things related to it
 
 
 1
 Two major parties of the Valley - National Conference (NC) and Peoples Democratic Party (PDP) have boycotted the elections
 2
 The Communist Party of india-marxist (CPI-M), the Peoples Democratic Front (PDF) led by Hakim Yasin and the Democratic Nationalist Party (DPN) headed by Ghulam Hasan Mir have also kept themselves away from elections
 3
 The Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP), Congress and independents are in the fray only
 4
 244 candidates have been elected unopposed, while no candidates are in the fray for 159 municipal wards of Kashmir
 5
 From the data point of view, 29 per cent of the voters in the valley have no candidate to elect in their wards
 6
 Election campaign was also not seen at any place in the valley
 7
 The terrorists have issued threats to both candidates and voters

 dakshin africa tej gendbaaj del sten ne series ke prati apni betaabi yah kahkar zaahir kii he ki vah apni indian premier lig (ipel) team ke captain shikhar dhawan ko apane khilaaf aazmaana chaahate hai

 lekin shikhar kii maujuuda form kii vajah se sten unke khilaaf gendbaazi karne ko chunauti maanate hai
